Hitler Calls for Equality in International Status, Wishes to Reconcile with France and Seek Peace Together, Germany is No Longer What It Was, and Opposition to Russia Remains Unchanged 19

Karlsruhe – Last night, 70 special trains carrying residents from areas such as Baden, where troops were heavily stationed in the Rhineland, entered Karlsruhe to listen to Hitler explain his peace plan. The German leader, after receiving a warm welcome from 70,000 people, stated that the first priority for Germany and France is to be on an absolutely equal footing. Only when they are equal can they respect each other. Germany has no intention of attacking France or Poland, so Germany has taken the treaties between France and Poland lightly. However, the mutual assistance agreement signed between France and Russia is different. The German people have experience with the meaning of communism and deeply know that any country that cannot defend itself to resist the aims of the Communist Party will suffer its scourge. The German leader went on to detail his proposal, which is to conclude a 25-year non-aggression pact and an air pact to replace the Locarno Pact, which is the greatest work that any German can do. He also said that Germany cannot often have someone who can contribute 25 years of peace to 67 million people. Finally, he said that the time has now come to accept Germany as an equal member of the community of nations. (Reuters dispatch, thirteenth)

Karlsruhe – German leader Hitler delivered a speech to 60,000 residents of the Rhineland today and warned the world that he has proposed a plan for the appeasement of Europe, and if it is rejected, he will never be willing to make any suggestions again. Mr. Hitler then attacked war with his determination to abandon the Locarno Pact and the Treaty of Versailles, but also said that Germany would not hesitate to go to war with other countries in order to seek equality. The reason why Germans regard war as terrible is not because Germans are afraid, but because if war breaks out, the whole world will suffer its poison. Now that he is calling loudly for peace, he must call loudly for international equality. Mr. Hitler compared Germany when the National Socialist Party seized power in 1933 with today's Germany, saying that today's Germany is the most peaceful country in the world. Mr. Hitler pointed to France, fourteen miles away, and told it that there are now two countries here, although there are all kinds of past hatreds, but they can all exist. They often meet with weapons, but their borders have only changed by fifty kilometers. If this situation continues, there is no way to resolve it. Reason should indicate the way to resolve it. Regarding the Franco-Soviet mutual assistance treaty, Mr. Hitler said that France had previously concluded alliances with Czechoslovakia and Poland, and Germany had never opposed them because it had no intention of provoking them. What does France want? We do not yet know. However, we have already known the ambitions of the Communist Party. We have already seen what it has done in Germany. Mr. Hitler continued, there are now millions of Frenchmen who are willing to live in harmony with the Germans, but communism is an ominous thing. Only with equality as the foundation can a new order in Europe be built. I have made new suggestions to the world, and the breadth of their content is rare. Neighboring countries may be able to calm down and work with us. This is our greatest hope. (National News dispatch, twelfth)

Karlsruhe – Hitler delivered an election speech here, with a very peaceful tone, roughly saying, "I do not want to celebrate military glory, because I have experienced this kind of hardship. Compared with international politicians and any soldiers, I have experienced quite a lot. I deeply feel that war is cruel and terrible, not because we are cowardly, but because war itself is cruel and terrible. They regard war as a good thing, not because they are brave, but because war can give them considerable benefits. I want to build a monument in the hearts of the people, but a peace monument is far better than a war victory tower. Now a 12-inch shell costs 3,000 marks. If I add another 1,500 marks, I can build a worker's house. If I launch a million of these shells, there will be no benefit, but the total value can build countless workers' houses." (National Press dispatch, twelfth)

Locarno Treaty Signatories Acknowledge German Breach of Contract; Germany Refuses to Withdraw Troops, Stiffening British Attitude; League of Nations Council Scheduled to Meet This Morning 20

London – Representatives of the Locarno Treaty signatory nations, namely Great Britain, France, Italy, and Belgium, held an important meeting here this afternoon, unanimously resolving that Germany’s reoccupation of the demilitarized Rhineland constitutes a clear violation of Articles 42 and 43 of the Treaty of Versailles and the Locarno Treaty. The League of Nations Council should be requested to declare this point. To facilitate a more detailed study of the situation arising from Germany’s actions, a small committee has been appointed and is scheduled to meet at 11:30 tomorrow morning. After the formal meeting this afternoon, key figures among the four nations’ representatives continued discussions with each other. The meeting was held in the old Cabinet room of the Foreign Office, the very room where the Locarno Treaty was signed by [Austen] Chamberlain in the past. It began at 5:17 PM and adjourned at 7:45 PM. The chief British representative was Foreign Secretary [Anthony] Eden, serving as chairman, along with Lord Privy Seal [Viscount] Halifax, Permanent Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs [Sir Robert] Vansittart; France was represented by Foreign Minister [Pierre-Étienne] Flandin; Belgium by Prime Minister [Paul van] Zeeland; both nations’ ambassadors to London also attended; Italy was represented by its ambassador to London, [Dino] Grandi. (Reuters, 12th)

London – It is reported that British Foreign Secretary Eden has met with the German Ambassador to Great Britain, informing him that Germany could still make a gesture to help resolve the current crisis. (Reuters, 13th)

Signatory Nations Continued Deliberations Yesterday

London – At 11:30 this morning, the chief representatives of the Locarno Treaty signatory nations gathered at the British Foreign Office, continuing discussions until 1:35 PM before adjourning. They are scheduled to reconvene at 5:00 PM. In addition to Foreign Secretary Eden, the British representatives also included Chancellor of the Exchequer [Neville] Chamberlain, a point of note. Others present were French Foreign Minister Flandin, Belgian Prime Minister Zeeland, and Italian Ambassador to Great Britain Grandi. (Reuters, 13th)

London – After the Locarno Treaty signatory nations’ meeting adjourned, French Foreign Minister Flandin emerged from the Foreign Office at 1:35 PM with a happy expression. Italian Ambassador Grandi followed, and both paused to pose for photographs at the request of journalists before getting into their cars to return to their residences, smiling. Belgian Prime Minister Zeeland left at the same time, followed by Lord Privy Seal Halifax, who went to 10 Downing Street to report to the Prime Minister, all appearing cheerful. (Havas, 13th)

London – A special dispatch from our correspondent states that the Locarno Treaty signatory nations’ meeting adjourned here today at 1:30 PM and is scheduled to reconvene at 5:00 PM at the Prime Minister’s residence. At that time, the representatives of Great Britain, France, Italy, and Belgium will decide on various specific measures to be presented to the League of Nations Council when it confirms tomorrow that Germany has violated the Treaty of Versailles (Articles 42 and 43) and the Locarno Treaty (Article 2). It is generally understood that Belgian Prime Minister Zeeland presented a motion at this afternoon’s meeting, which will serve as the basis for discussions at the Locarno Treaty signatory nations’ meeting this afternoon. (Havas, 13th)

League of Nations Meeting Procedures Today

London – The situation in Europe is considered very serious here, as France is determined to deal with Germany’s abrogation of treaties in a stern manner. It is expected that tomorrow’s meeting of the League of Nations Council will be merely a formality and will not immediately discuss fundamental issues. Tomorrow’s procedure will be nothing more than recording Germany’s breach of the Locarno Treaty and appointing a committee to discuss and report on how to address the problem. This report will be sent to the Locarno Treaty signatory nations, after which the representatives of the countries concerned will hold several decisive meetings and private talks. (Reuters, 13th)

London – The League of Nations Council is scheduled to meet here tomorrow. The venue has been selected as the “Queen Anne Room” on the second floor of St. James’s Palace. This room is of great historical value. From this morning, palace staff have been busy cleaning, with a high degree of tension. The adjoining room, known as the “Ante-Room,” will be reserved for secretaries and typists. The room is equipped with a horseshoe-shaped conference table, around which the representatives of each nation will sit during the meeting. The floor is covered with a red carpet to protect the antique holly wood flooring. Firewood is burning in the fireplaces to maintain a suitable temperature. Meanwhile, specialists dispatched by the Post Office are busy installing telegraph and telephone lines (a total of 200 lines) for use by the national representatives and journalists. (Havas, 13th)

A Strong Atmosphere for Sanctions Against Germany

London – Europe today is close to a major conflict. The foreign ministers of ten nations are awaiting the meeting of the League of Nations Council in an atmosphere of extreme tension. As the meeting approaches, the possibility of imposing economic sanctions on Germany seems to have become more likely. A leading British financier told the Associated Press that he believes war with Germany is very possible. Diplomatic circles, however, remain rather detached, not believing in talk of war. However, the united front against Germany has greatly solidified. According to Berlin sources, the German government is very uneasy about sanctions, as the implementation of sanctions may lead to an economic blockade and a boycott of German goods. At the same time, British sentiment has gradually shifted toward France. Public opinion in official and public circles has always sought compromise, but after hearing the speeches of German Chancellor [Adolf] Hitler and Prussian Prime Minister and Minister of Aviation [Hermann] Göring, it has turned tough. (Guomin, 12th)

German Note Replies to Great Britain; Rejects Troop Withdrawal Suggestion 21

Opposition to Limiting Sovereignty Along the Rhine, Whether Temporarily or Permanently

London – German Ambassador to Great Britain [Leopold von] Hoesch recently delivered a note from his government to Foreign Secretary Eden, stating in essence: "Germany cannot participate in any negotiations that would limit Germany's sovereignty along the Rhine River, regardless of whether the limitation is temporary or permanent. To facilitate the French government’s acceptance of Germany’s proposal, our Chancellor ([Adolf] Hitler referring to himself) wishes to clarify his intention from the outset, namely that Germany’s restoration of its original sovereignty along the Rhine River should only have symbolic significance at this time. The number of troops stationed in several towns along the Rhine River is based on peacetime levels and has been communicated to the military attachés of the British and French embassies in Germany. These numbers will not be increased. Germany does not intend to move these troops closer to the borders of Belgium and France at this time. Both of these measures will be observed during the current negotiations, provided that Belgium and France adopt the same attitude." According to reports, Foreign Secretary Eden asked German Ambassador Hoesch yesterday to convey to his government that “the current situation is extremely serious, and the German government should voluntarily express its sincerity in seeking a compromise to facilitate future negotiations. Is it possible to take ‘symbolic’ action by withdrawing some troops stationed along the Rhine River and at least refraining from increasing the number of stationed troops during the negotiations?” The German note is a response to the questions raised by Foreign Secretary Eden. After the Locarno Treaty signatory nations’ meeting adjourned today, Foreign Secretary Eden, French Foreign Minister Flandin, Belgian Prime Minister Zeeland, and Italian Ambassador Grandi held a secret meeting to discuss the situation. At this time, the delegations of Belgium, France, and Italy remained silent regarding the German reply, while the British Foreign Office has released the contents of the reply to the newspapers. It is generally believed that the British Cabinet, in light of the difficult situation in the reconciliation efforts, should allow public opinion to understand this, so the German reply was released. (Havas, 12th)

Shift in British Attitude 22

No Longer Accommodating Germany, Paris Greatly Relieved

London – The representatives of the Locarno Treaty nations, gathered here this afternoon, were deeply dissatisfied with [Adolf] Hitler’s disregard for the suggestion of British Foreign Secretary [Anthony] Eden, viewing it as mockery of Britain’s moderate attitude towards Germany. The French representatives recognized this as a challenge from the Germans. A British spokesperson told an Associated Press reporter that Britain would no longer adopt an accommodating attitude towards Germany. At the same time, members of the British Conservative Party are pressuring diplomatic authorities to actively cooperate with France and Belgium. According to another report, [Winston] Churchill, [Lord] Hailsham, and [Neville] Chamberlain have all called on the nation to be loyal to the obligations of the Locarno Treaty. (Guomin, 12th)

London – Since Germany’s abrogation of the Locarno Treaty last Saturday, France has been in a state of anxiety every day. Only today does it feel relieved, as the British government has deemed Germany’s recent proposals unsatisfactory and has adopted a firm stance. People in Paris have been greatly impressed by this. According to French opinion, peace can only be achieved through close cooperation between Britain and France. (Reuters, 13th)

Distinguished Guests Gather in London 23

To Attend the League of Nations Council Meeting

London – The League of Nations Council is scheduled to hold a meeting here on Saturday (i.e., the 14th) at 11:00 AM. League of Nations Secretary-General [Joseph] Avenol, Romanian Foreign Minister [Nicolae] Titulescu, and Soviet Commissar for Foreign Affairs [Maxim] Litvinov all arrived here this afternoon to attend the Council meeting. (Havas, 12th)

London – The League of Nations Council will still hold its meeting as originally planned at 11:00 AM on Saturday at St. James’s Palace to consider the European crisis caused by Germany’s unilateral abrogation of the Locarno Treaty. League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol arrived here yesterday with a large staff to prepare for the meeting. British Foreign Secretary [Anthony] Eden had suggested to Germany that, while negotiating a new treaty to replace the Locarno Treaty, it should withdraw all troops from the demilitarized Rhineland area, leaving only a "symbolic" number. This proposal has been rejected by Germany. Therefore, the meeting that day is very important, not only to declare Germany’s violation of the Locarno Treaty, but also to ask it to propose suggestions to adapt to the situation. It is widely rumored that a special committee will be organized to study the issue, and representatives from Denmark, Portugal, Spain, Turkey, and South American countries will also be invited to join the committee. The meeting may last for a week.

The committee will propose suggestions based on Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant (which stipulates that any member of the League may withdraw from the League after giving two years’ prior notice, but must, at the time of withdrawal, fulfill all its international obligations and all obligations under this Covenant), and the Council will notify Germany. If Germany ignores this, the Council will have no choice but to convene a general meeting of the League of Nations to hold an extraordinary meeting to decide on actions to take against Germany. French circles now feel that the time has come to discuss the scope of mutual assistance that should be available, and the circumstances in which such mutual assistance should be provided. The French firmly declare that France has never refused to discuss the abolition of the demilitarized zone, and has never regarded this zone as permanent, but only discusses it under the force of accomplished facts. France should refuse. It is said that several countries agree with the attitude held by France. (Reuters, 13th)

Berlin Issues Communiqué Criticizing Franco-Soviet Pact 24

If Peace Plans Are Not Considered, Germany Prefers Isolated Self-Defense

London – Berlin issued a communiqué last night stating that if the peace proposals made by [Adolf] Hitler and the reasons for Germany’s abrogation of the Locarno Treaty are not sympathetically considered by other countries, then Germany will abandon its peace efforts and resort to isolated self-defense. French sources in London described this as an attempt by Germany to put pressure on the London negotiations, but did not consider it important, as a breakdown in the London discussions would ultimately leave Germany isolated. The Berlin communiqué first criticized France’s plans to guarantee its security, stating that before the establishment of the Locarno Treaty, France had already concluded military alliances with Belgium, Czechoslovakia, and Poland. These alliances were described as defensive in nature, and since Germany had no aggressive intentions, Germany did not oppose these alliances. For the same reason, Germany did not object to France’s massive concentration of troops and construction of fortifications along its borders after the war. As for the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact, its nature is truly peculiar, as Russia is committed to world revolution and has declared a program of blatant imperialism and aggression. France already has Great Britain, Belgium, Poland, Czechoslovakia, and Italy as guarantors of its security, yet it still needs the support of a huge Russia. At that time, Germany had not taken any action to harm France. Before concluding the Franco-Soviet Pact, France did not notify the signatories of the Locarno Treaty. France’s self-defense plans are very thorough, yet it is now said that the nineteen battalions of German troops sent into the Rhineland will endanger the security guaranteed by half the world. On the one hand, Germany is only occupying its own land with a small number of troops in order to reduce France’s fear and induce France to join negotiations. On the other hand, Germany is also making a great contribution to seeking peace. If its proposal for a twenty-five-year non-aggression pact is accepted by other countries, it will be the first universal European pact after the Treaty of Versailles, without discriminatory measures. When the Franco-Soviet Pact made the Locarno Treaty ineffective, Germany could have declared the direct military occupation of the Rhineland, but Germany did not do so. Instead, it preferred to propose a grand peace plan and limit the rearmament of the Rhineland to a symbolic form. Germany is prepared not to increase its troops stationed in the Rhineland during negotiations, provided that France and Belgium take the same action, but Germany will never give up any part of its sovereignty. Germany firmly believes that a future peace obtained through forced discrimination will sow the seeds of dishonor on the one hand and leave behind latent hatred on the other. Germany is committed to establishing a genuine peace in Europe for the next twenty-five years based on the equal freedom of decision of peoples and nations. (Reuters, 13th)

Paris – Foreign Minister [Pierre-Étienne] Flandin, when talking with guests today about the communiqué released by Berlin yesterday, said that France maintains a firm attitude while retaining its measured optimism, and that the German communiqué is an attempt to preempt negotiations. At the same time, French political circles declared that the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact is not a military alliance. (Reuters, 13th)

German Land and Air Forces Sufficient to Resist Any Aggression 25

A Boastful Statement by the Minister of Aviation

Berlin – Minister of Aviation [Hermann] Göring said in an election campaign speech in Königsberg today that Germany’s military strength is sufficient to resist any aggression against Germany. Today, there is no road, land, or sky that can allow troops to invade Berlin. However, Germany’s armament does not threaten any country. Germany took a great step on February 7th. No matter what happens, Germany intends to defend its rights and will never waver. (Reuters, 13th)

Germany’s Treaty-Breaking Actions May Have Been Prompted by Financial Panic; Diverting People’s Attention Outward; Currency Devaluation Inevitable 26

Experienced observers in the Swiss capital recently expressed the opinion that German Chancellor [Adolf] Hitler’s abrogation of the Locarno Treaty was in fact prompted by the country’s financial situation. The government, facing an inevitable currency devaluation, drafted a large-scale plan for financial and economic reform. Hitler also reoccupied the Rhineland area to divert people’s attention. Once the results of the Reichstag elections are announced and the government achieves victory, it will implement currency devaluation. The Neue Zürcher Zeitung reported, "[Adolf] Hitler asked the people of his country for the necessary assistance when he announced the Reichstag elections would be held on the 29th of this month, in order to seek economic benefits. It can be seen that the talk of devaluation of the Mark is not groundless." (Havas, 13th)

British Army Mechanization; Preparing to Participate in European Land Wars; Supporting Collective Security and Jointly Resisting Aggression; Secretary of State for War Explains Reasons for Increased Budget 27

London – Secretary of State for War [Alfred Duff] Cooper declared during the debate on the army budget in the House of Commons today that the British Army will soon have the best anti-tank weapons in the world. The army budget for 1936 totals £49,201,000, an increase of £5,730,000 compared to last year, of which £1,555,000 is due to the special plans taken regarding the Italo-Abyssinian War. The budget does not stipulate the acceleration and expansion of defense contemplated in the recent government white paper. Cooper told the House of Commons that the Army Department has decided to adopt two new weapons: an anti-tank rifle and an anti-tank machine gun, which will be issued to the troops as soon as possible. He also said that the British Army will add two new tank battalions, and eight cavalry regiments are currently being mechanized. The existing tank brigades will be combined with the mechanized cavalry brigades to form guerrilla divisions. The infantry is also being reorganized, with three rifle battalions combined with one machine gun battalion, equipped with new anti-tank weapons and new reconnaissance vehicles. In his speech, Cooper mentioned that it is often heard that if Britain participates in a European war again, it should only assist with its navy and air force. Although it would greatly relieve the Army Council if this could be decided early, those responsible for the army believe that they can hardly proceed on any such conjecture. He said he could not determine whether Britain would not send a well-equipped army to Europe on very short notice in a future war. If Britain participates in a European war, it should support the policy advocated by the majority of the British people, namely collective security. If Britain’s assistance is indeed limited to naval and air force warfare, then other partners in the collective security system will be greatly disappointed. A Member of Parliament asked if British forces could be deployed to Europe in time to assist a country under aggression. Cooper replied that this could be answered in two ways: if any country that Britain needs to assist knows that Britain will send a large army to help, it will have a great impact on the country’s entire military strategy at the beginning of the war and make the country’s fighting spirit stronger. The speed of mobilization of land forces is constantly increasing. (Reuters, 13th)

French Senate Passes Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact; Effective Immediately Upon Presidential Signature 28

Paris – The Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact, which had already been passed by the Chamber of Deputies, was passed by the Senate today by a vote of 231 to 52.

It is said that Germany abrogated the Locarno Treaty on the pretext that this pact endangers its security. The pact contains a protocol of five articles based on Articles 10, 15, and 16 of the League of Nations Covenant and stipulates that mutual assistance should be provided in the event of unprovoked aggression by another country. (Reuters, 16th)

Paris – Following the Chamber of Deputies, the Senate approved the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty by a vote of 233 to 52. The treaty will take effect as soon as it is signed by the President. At the meeting today, Senator Bérenger, chairman of the Senate Foreign Affairs Committee, first stood up to speak, urging senators to immediately reject motions to postpone the discussion, as opponents of the treaty may propose such motions, and said that the treaty should be approved immediately after German Chancellor [Adolf] Hitler abrogated the Locarno Treaty. Subsequently, senators opposed to the treaty spoke one after another, explaining the reasons why they could not approve it. Finally, [Henry] de Jouvenel, the rapporteur of the Foreign Affairs Committee, presented a report explaining the three reasons on which it was based, saying that “Germany’s abrogation of the Locarno Treaty is clearly a provocative action.” The approval motion was then put to a vote and passed by a large majority. Tokyo, Jiji Newspaper reported this morning that the Hirota Cabinet's basic diplomatic policy will undoubtedly be the implementation of an independent and active continental policy. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs also believes that the background of this policy is the enhancement of national defense, and it agrees to focus on Japan's military preparations in Manchuria. Although there are fears that Japan's international relations will be disturbed by this, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that without this policy, there will be no way to adjust Japan's relations with Russia and China. Since Soviet Russia has not expressed its intention to withdraw its Far East military preparations, the Japanese government has no choice but to consider increasing its troop strength in Manchuria to match the strength of the Russian army in the Far East in order to prevent border disputes and adjust the relationship between Japan, "Manchuria," and Russia. It is expected that this policy will change China's attitude toward Japan. This is because British and American interests in China are only related to economic expansion and development, while Japan's interests in China are necessary for the survival of the Japanese people and indispensable for the development of the Japanese nation. Therefore, Japan must create a situation in which British and American economic interests in China must be expanded only after obtaining Japan's understanding. (Reuters dispatch on the 13th)

Tokyo, The new cabinet's program and policies are scheduled to be decided and announced at today's regular cabinet meeting. At today's cabinet meeting, Baba, chairman of the policy proposal drafting committee, will report on the research process. Currently, only the policy programs submitted by the various ministries are being reviewed. After the draft decision is submitted and passed at the regular cabinet meeting on the 17th, it will be approved and announced on the same day. (Dentsu dispatch on the 13th)

The army authorities plan to incorporate policies that have been studied for many years into the demands to be implemented by the Hirota Cabinet. The specific contents are roughly as follows:

"Establish a guiding spirit for determining national policy." Since the Manchurian Incident, Japan's international status has risen, and the entire nation has entered an era of great advancement. However, political, economic, and other systems still maintain their old state. Internal and external policies have been passive and regressive until today. Now that the new cabinet has been established, it should adopt a new spirit, abandon the attitude of maintaining the status quo or being passive, and reform various policies to establish active policies in order to develop national fortunes.

"Substantial national defense and adjust national defense capabilities." To seek trade development and establish overseas markets, it is necessary to first strengthen national defense to avoid being intimidated by other countries, which is an absolute prerequisite. Therefore, based on Japan's current objective situation and the situations it will inevitably encounter in the future, it is necessary to establish maximum national defense capabilities with minimum military expenditures. For this purpose, establish the fundamentals of national policy, and the army and navy should cooperate to allow the organic performance of national defense capabilities to operate freely.

"Establish diplomatic policies and adjust the fundamentals of national policy and national defense capabilities. At the same time, actively use foreign policies as an urgent task at present."

"Decisively reform the administrative structure." Renovate the administrative structure and eliminate the departmentalism of various ministries. This will nurture national strength and stabilize the lives of the people. If necessary, implement the abolition or merger of various ministries, and limit the number of state ministers to a small number whose mission is to implement national policy, while officials in each ministry manage routine affairs.

"Decisively implement tax increases and reform the economic structure. It is absolutely necessary to reorganize the tax system to ensure the average burden on the people. In the future, as national expenditures expand, it will be unavoidable to decisively implement tax increases to make up for the lack of revenue. However, the method and timing of its implementation must be carefully considered. In addition, the unreasonable and unrestrained economic structure should be given considerable rationalization, reform, and control, otherwise all national policies will become empty words. (Domei dispatch on the 13th)

Scientific Conversations

Edited by the Science Society of China 40

— Xingcun

Factors Affecting Insect Occurrence Insect occurrence

is always limited by environmental factors. Some say that the factors affecting

insect occurrence belong to the climate aspect.

Generally, people believe that the number of insects occurring in a certain period

depends entirely on whether the climate is suitable or not. Others

say that the factors limiting insect occurrence are biological aspects,

that is, the number of insects occurring depends entirely on

the number of natural enemies. The so-called natural enemies include

beneficial birds, beneficial insects, and beneficial animals, all of which

use pests as food. When talking about biological factors, we

think of a "natural balance" phenomenon in nature.

That is, nature often maintains a certain number of

animals to prevent them from suddenly increasing. For example,

there is often a pest that, in its place of origin, is able to maintain natural

balance and not cause great harm due to the limitations of parasitic

insects or other natural enemies. Once it leaves its

place of origin and moves to another place, then in the new environment,

due to the lack of natural enemies, it cannot maintain natural

balance. As a result, the number of individuals increases sharply and becomes a major problem.

Modern economic entomologists are advocating the biological pest

control method, that is, using this method to implement insect control

by insects, often introducing the natural enemies of pests

from very far away to kill pests. Pest control in various countries

has also achieved considerable success in this aspect.

The Periodicity of Locust Occurrence Locusts are an important pest

of crops in our country, but they do not cause harm every year.

They must be separated by several years before causing harm. Therefore, locust

occurrence is periodic. Entomologists have an explanation for this

phenomenon, that is, locusts can be divided into gregarious

and solitary types. These two types are not only obviously different in morphology,

but also have different habits. Gregarious types

can migrate in groups over long distances and cause great harm. This is the so-called

"flying locusts covering the sky." All the flying locusts that feed on crops

belong to this type. Solitary locusts mostly live scattered

and do not need to migrate in groups over long distances, so they do not cause disasters. In fact, gregarious

and solitary types can change interactively. When the

environment is suitable and food is abundant, solitary types can

become gregarious types. Conversely, when the environment is unsuitable and food

is lacking, gregarious types can also become solitary types.

Therefore, years in which locusts do not cause great harm do not mean that

there are no locusts at all during that period. However, at that time, solitary

locusts did not become gregarious flying locusts.

Pest Occurrence Prediction In pest control methods,

there is an ideal method that has not yet been completely successful,

that is, trying to predict the occurrence of pests in advance,

just like weather stations predict wind and rain. In this way,

pests can be prevented in advance and achieve twice the result with half the effort.

However, actually predicting pest occurrence is not as

simple as predicting the climate, because in addition to climate factors,

there are also biological factors

affecting insect occurrence. Climate factors include temperature, rainfall, etc.

Therefore, entomologists, although having great

aspirations in this area, have not yet achieved complete success.

If we want to use meteorological records to predict

the occurrence of a pest, we must first understand the average

temperature and average humidity or average rainfall of the pest's occurrence area.

(The average for the month or the year is determined as needed.) According to the research of Mr. Cai Banghua, the striped stem borer

(the striped stem borer is one of the important pests in rice-producing areas in our country. During its larval stage, it specializes in drilling into the rice

stems and gnawing on the tissues inside the rice stems, resulting in dead heart

seedlings and white ears, which are extremely difficult to eliminate). In Hangzhou

Xianqiao, if the climate in August and September of the first year

is high in temperature and high in rainfall, then the number of striped

stem borer individuals born in the second year will definitely be very large, and the degree of harm

to rice will also definitely be very high. The reason is that the

climate with high temperature and high rainfall in August and September is extremely suitable for

the reproduction of striped stem borers. Therefore, striped stem borers usually

occur only three times in Hangzhou Xianqiao, but when this

type of climate occurs, it can increase to four times. Since it occurs

once more, the number of overwintering larvae also increases

accordingly. Therefore, the striped stem borer in that area in the second year shows a large-scale

occurrence phenomenon and becomes rampant. Therefore, if we

want to predict the occurrence of the striped stem borer in the second year, we can

create a climate map of the average temperature and average

rainfall recorded each month of the previous year and compare it with the climate map

of the normal occurrence year of the striped stem borer (that is, the year when the striped stem borer is not rampant),

then it will not be difficult to predict it.

Legislative Yuan Holds Routine Meeting and Passes Regulations on Cracking Down on Adulteration of Water and Impurities in Cotton 46

Nanjing, The Legislative Yuan held its 51st meeting on the morning of the 13th, attended by 64 members, including Legislator Han Xuan and others. Sun Ke presided, and Liang Hancao was the Secretary-General. They passed the revised Provisional Regulations on Cracking Down on Adulteration of Water and Impurities in Cotton. The regulations were formulated and promulgated in July 23. Since their implementation, the National Economic Commission, based on the resolutions of the previous National Cotton Inspection Administrative Conference, believed that the original regulations still had shortcomings, such as the lack of a clear definition of the highest limit for impurities, and that mixing cotton was seriously related to the quality of cotton, such as mixing American cotton seeds into Chinese cotton seeds, resulting in mixed varieties, and mixing coarse-fiber cotton with fine-fiber cotton, causing disorder of product grades. The original regulations also lacked punitive provisions, so a revised bill was drafted and sent to the Executive Yuan, which ordered the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to review it. After the Central Political Council reviewed the opinions, it was transferred to the Legislative Yuan for review. After the Commercial Law Committee and the Economic Committee of the Legislative Yuan reviewed the bill, they revised it according to the original plan. The main points of the revision are: the statutory standard for domestic cotton is 11% moisture content and 0.05% impurity content. The highest limit for moisture content and impurity content for buying and selling in the market is 12% and 2%, respectively. If the moisture content and impurity content exceed the highest limit, buying and selling will be suspended, but this does not apply to those with high impurity content and unsuitable for sorting. Anyone who adulterates water and impurities in cotton with the intention of seeking illegal profits shall be sentenced to imprisonment of not more than three years, detention, or a fine of not more than 1,000 yuan, or both. Those who mix cotton seeds and cotton types shall also be fined not more than 1,000 yuan. Export cotton shall be handled in accordance with the Commodity Inspection Law. (Central News Agency telegram on the 13th)

Western Border Communications

Travel Notes in Qinghai (Continued) 81

— Zhuang Xueben

A separate page should be dedicated to narrating the history of our host, the Tusi Li, and his lineage of Li Keyong.

His ancestor was Zhu Xie Zhiyi, the chieftain of the Shatuo tribe in the Western Regions during the reign of Emperor Xianzong of the Tang Dynasty. After assisting the Tang Dynasty, his son Ping Pangdong made meritorious contributions. He was granted the name Li Guochang and made Jiedushi of Datong. He had a son, Keyong, who destroyed Huang Chao and was enfeoffed as the Prince of Jin. He had thirteen sons: commonly known as the Thirteen Taibao. His son, Cunxu, destroyed Zhu Liang and became Emperor Zhuangzong of the Later Tang Dynasty. Siyuan became Emperor Mingzong of the Later Tang Dynasty. During the Song Dynasty, his descendants Jigong and Jipeng were Jiedushi. During the Yuan Dynasty, Li Shangge was the Prince of Qi's Mansion. His son, Meidegu, was granted land at Hongyagou Beichuan Shiguanzhuang. Meidegu's son was Nange. In the Yuan Dynasty, he was the Vice Magistrate of Xining Prefecture. In the Ming Dynasty, he advanced to the rank of Commander, awarded the title of Earl of Huining posthumously. He had one son: Li Ying, Li Xiong. Li Ying was promoted to Guanglu Dafu Zhuguo, Earl of Huining for his military exploits. His descendants inherited the title of Eastern Earl's Mansion and lived in Shangchuankou, 120 miles southeast of Nianbo County. Li Xiong advanced to Ronglu Dafu Zhuguo, Earl of Gaoyang. He also inherited the title and called it the Western Earl's Mansion, living in Qitacheng, 30 miles south of Xining County. Both had land and people under their jurisdiction, with 23 Qianbabzong under them, and 23 extra deputy posts, 300 local soldiers. In the second year of the Shunzhi reign of the Qing Dynasty, Li Zhen of the Eastern Earl's Mansion and Li Tianyu of the Western Earl's Mansion surrendered simultaneously and were granted the title of Commander Tongzhi.

Tusi Li inherited a branch of the Eastern Earl's Mansion, so his current card still has the title "Nianbo South Hereditary Tusi Commander Tongzhi" printed on it. During the previous Qing Dynasty, the organization of the Tusi Yamen had one Qianzong, two Babzongs, four Waiwei, one hundred Qianhus, two Baihus, and 300 local soldiers. The local soldiers were based on the Tuntian system, completing orders while integrating soldiers with agriculture. Since the Republic of China, the Tusi system has been replaced by the Liuguan system, and the Tusi has lost his power; however, the people still have a hereditary respect for those in office. The former Tusi of the Western Earl's Mansion was named Li Peilin, and he currently lives in Xining.

After arriving at Sangsige, the first feeling was that the men's and women's clothing was more distinctive.

The difference in women's headdresses and men's clothing is small. They wear faceless sheepskin jackets, belts, lambskin hats, soft boots, and some have a fire pot hanging in between. However, every local also drags a long braid.

Women's clothing is usually a brown cloth shirt. During these few New Years, many wear a new garment with five-colored sleeves: the outer garment is a black robe, and the sleeves are made of two-inch red, yellow, blue, purple, and green cloth strips, sewn into two beautiful sleeves. The rich wear a green silk or black velvet short vest, with four large ruyi patterns inlaid on the front and back corners of the clothing. Two strings of fine, red-and-white beads are hung around the neck, with earrings hanging down to the shoulders. The shoes have double straps, made of red, yellow, and green cloth strips. Unmarried women have bald heads and wear two braids. Married women wear two types of headdresses: a three-pronged head and a dry food head.

The "three-pronged head" is also known as the "pointed head," with a Shagol covering the back of the head. It is connected to twenty or thirty three-inch-long copper tubes, tied into an oval shape with red rope, and a copper arrow is inserted on top; it rises about half a foot above the top of the head, with the arrowhead divided into three prongs, with two small red velvet balls hanging on it. Several red ropes are suspended from the braids, and a circular (he ga), half a foot in diameter, is dragged on the back, tilted upwards, made of red paperboard, and the front is made of five-colored beads as small as rice grains, arranged into nine-colored circles, with a white small conch shell inlaid around the outside. The "dry food head" is also known as the "sesame cake head," with a circular red paperboard, shaped like a sesame cake, inserted on the head, with the local name Tokuila. Red rope is nailed on the edge, hanging down. Tassels are used, and the back is lined with colored lace silk. A raised Chelga is also dragged on the back.

This type of headdress is completely different from that of Tangba Fort. Men's clothing is made of brown cloth in summer, and women wear cloth.

The degree of Han Chinese influence on the locals is not deep here. They have dangerous-looking faces and beautiful valleys, and their actions are very genuine. The women are petite, and the men are strong. They have not seen photography before, so when I take pictures of them, their postures are very lively and natural. A few local women who know a little cleanliness rub a red color like rouge on their already washed faces. This makes their apple-colored faces look more Kangfo and beautiful.

The wind here is also very lively. Leaning on the mountains on the left, there are valleys nearby. Along the road and the bank of the ditch are neat and slender white poplars, and the Pengkang at the corner of the road gives people the feeling of being in a garden. The Hongyazi Ditch is now frozen with thick ice, and a row of five or six water mills adorn the great river ditch: the creaking sound of the machines and the constantly rotating wheels are very good at stimulating the poetic mood of tourists. When the rising sun rises, and when the setting sun is about to set, women wearing five-colored clothes drive a flock of sheep and bring several livestock, walking through the woods. They shout by the riverside! The calls of cattle and sheep drinking water, the golden waves are shaking, and the heavy father leisurely returns to the forest. A row of women carrying water buckets appear by the river one after another, chatting and laughing, the sunlight shining on their hat crowns, coming and going endlessly, until the sun rises three poles high, or the new moon is in the forest, and their shadows also disappear with it.

One Yuan per Mu of Land

The lives of the locals are characterized by female diligence and male laziness. During these few New Year's days, the men do even less work, idling around in the courtyards all day long. Although the women should also rest and enjoy themselves, they are still busy carrying water, carrying manure, herding sheep, and collecting cow dung all day long.

The local customs are purer here; therefore, they carry water like the Westerners. A tall bucket is tied with two ropes, the ropes are placed on the left and right shoulders, and the water bucket stands steadily on the back.

Their dwellings also have two-story buildings.

They are all very struggling economically, and there is even less cash in circulation. Few well-off locals can take out ten silver dollars from their homes. The interest rate they borrow from the lamas is as high as 5%.

The terrain is 2,840 meters high. The climate in the valley is relatively warm, and crops can be planted after Qingming. There are a total of thirty households in the village, and Han Chinese account for one-tenth of them. Most of them also grow a few dou of crops and raise a few sheep.

Most of them are self-sufficient, so prices are very low; land is one yuan per mu, and the highest is no more than six yuan, horses are twenty to one hundred yuan. Mules are around one hundred yuan, cattle are ten to twenty yuan. Sheep are two yuan. Pigs are six yuan, green fruits are one yuan per dou. Wheat is one yuan five jiao per dou. Beans are two yuan per dou.

Marriage at Seven Years Old

Marriage customs are more free here than in other places. Usually, if a man and woman are in love, they give gifts and worship heaven and earth, and they can formally become husband and wife.

However, authoritarian marriage is still prevalent. Well-off families practice the system of young husbands and old wives, often marrying a seven or eight-year-old child to a twenty-year-old daughter-in-law. Because the local women are diligent in labor and the men are idle and do not engage in production, the purpose of the young husband and old wife system is not to have children, but to help the husband's family manage agricultural affairs. This type of daughter-in-law does not worship in the hall when she comes through the door. Only the husband's family pays the wedding gift.

The wedding gift is sent to the woman's family before the formal marriage: one horse, one cow, one hybrid cow, ten bolts of brown cloth, sixteen pieces of cloth, and eighty strings of money. Depending on the wealth of the man's family, the wedding gift may be slightly increased or decreased.

For the wedding, the Lama chooses an auspicious day to pick up the bride. Enter the kitchen, wear a dry food head or a two-pronged head, the husband and wife worship the hall, relatives sit around the courtyard and drink and chat.

The conclusion of their marriages does not take into account bloodlines or seniority. Close relatives are not allowed. It is also very common for widows to remarry. There are very few marriages between Han Chinese and locals. When there are, it is only locals marrying Han Chinese.

Because the wedding gifts demanded by the woman's family are very heavy, many poor men never have a wife in their lives. Many women are also unable to marry and die old in their mother's homes. Sex is inevitable for bachelors and spinsters. Because their sexual problems are very public, things like running away together become much less common.

Fifteen-Year-Old Ah Gu

When unmarried women reach the age of fifteen, they kneel down to their parents, heaven and earth, and connect the ends of the two braids on their back, and they are called "wearing the heaven head." From then on, they are envied and called "Ah Gu."

"Ah Gu" can enjoy the right to freedom in love. Parents and siblings cannot interfere. She is still working in her mother's house anyway. It is very free for Ah Gu to find a lover outside or bring a lover home. If she brings a man of good reputation home, her parents and siblings are also willing to help her entertain him. If Ah Gu has children, they are considered children of the mother's family, and have the mother's family name, and Ah Gu will die old in her mother's family. If Ah Gu's lover gives a wedding gift and takes her away, it is up to her whether she wants to take the children with her or not. The children who are not taken are regarded as descendants of the maternal family.

There are also a small number of Ah Gu who, because they have too many lovers, are unable to extricate themselves from the sea of love. They wear a headdress and live in their mother's home in order to cope with it. Therefore, there are indeed many bachelors and spinsters among the locals who do not marry, but in fact most of them are neither bachelors nor spinsters.

It is said that their local lascivious atmosphere is because there are two mountains in Ledu County in front, and a stream flows between them that looks too much like a woman's private parts, so it has destroyed their feng shui.

When a man decides on a wife, he sends the wedding gift over, and the woman's family accepts it: her lover will make him a silk collar, embroidered with beautiful patterns of red and green silk threads and purple copper wire, and sew it on her fiancé's brown cloth clothing to show that it is a gift of their engagement. So, if you want to know whether a young man is engaged or not, you just need to see if he has a flower collar around his neck.

Inland and Foreign Goods Intermodal Transportation Set to Commence on May 1st 82

Tianjin Dispatch: Regarding the intermodal transportation of goods between inland and foreign territories, following the realization of the railway traffic, the Japanese side had hoped to continue its implementation. However, both sides were engaged in negotiations and discussions. After Yin Tong was appointed as Director of the Beining Railway Bureau, he went to Dalian to discuss the details with the Kwantung Army and the South Manchuria Railway Company, seeking to reconcile opinions. No immediate agreement was reached. Last year, after Takeshita Yoshii succeeded Ise Makoto as the chief of the Kwantung Army's Yuguan Special Service Organ, he also strove to revive the matter. Usami Hiroshi, the Director of the Railway Department of the South Manchuria Railway, came to Pingjin last winter to promote the issue, but ultimately, due to numerous complexities, it was difficult to realize. Recently, the Beining Railway Bureau, the South Manchuria Railway Bureau, and relevant parties of the Kwantung Railway General Bureau, feeling the practical needs, have taken a business-oriented stance and jointly sought technical cooperation. Previously, Usami Hiroshi, Director of the South Manchuria Railway and concurrently Director of the Railway General Bureau, dispatched Sakai Seibei as a representative to Tianjin to negotiate a compromise with Chen Juesheng, Director of the Beining Railway Bureau. On March 6th, at 10 a.m., at the Beining Reception Office on Avenue Joffre in the French Concession of Tianjin, they, along with Takeshita, the chief of the Yuguan Special Service Organ, who was also present, concluded an intermodal transportation agreement and supplementary articles regarding account settlement, etc. It is scheduled to commence on May 1st. According to the Beining Railway Bureau, the agreement was based on principled discussions, so the results obtained are considered satisfactory. The essential points of the intermodal transportation agreement are recorded below:

* This intermodal transportation of goods is limited to the lines of the Chinese state-owned Beining Railway, the South Manchuria Railway Company, and the Kwantung Railway General Bureau. The names of the stations that handle this intermodal transportation of goods will be announced by both parties.

* For both full carload and less-than-full carload shipments accepted for this intermodal transportation of goods, the railway will be responsible. A waybill or delivery order will be issued at the originating station and will be valid directly to the destination station, without the need for re-ticketing at each connecting railway. All goods passing through Shanhaiguan Station will generally be transferred at that station, unloaded by the delivering railway and loaded by the receiving railway. The freight charges will be calculated according to the tariff rates of each railway, and the regulations of each railway will apply separately.

* The formats of all required waybills, delivery orders, and other documents, as well as procedures for customs declaration and tax payment on behalf of merchants, advance payment of miscellaneous fees, currency exchange rates, and the settlement of accounts and disbursement of payments between the railways, have been determined in the "Intermodal Transportation Goods Account Settlement Method" and will be handled accordingly. Regarding direct communication between China and Japan, preparations are being actively made. More than ten telegraph operators have been transferred from the Ministry to Tianjin. Now that the ice has melted at Dagu and ships can enter the port, the equipment will be transported here within days. After installation and successful testing, telegrams between Tokyo and Tianjin can be sent directly without having to be relayed through the Shanghai International Radio Station, which is much more convenient than before. (11th)

Hangzhou Banking and Financial Industries Oppose Reorganization of Zhejiang Province's Debt - Issuance of New Provincial Bonds to Redeem Old Debts, Reduce Interest Rates, and Extend Repayment Periods 83

Hangzhou Dispatch: Cheng Yuanfan, the Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance, believes that the province's finances have reached a state of extreme difficulty. The provincial treasury owes more than 50 million yuan, and the principal and interest payments due each year exceed 5 million yuan, accounting for one-quarter of the province's income. Therefore, in order to reorganize the finances, it is necessary to start with the reorganization of debts. He has formulated a plan to reissue a large amount of public bonds, redeem the existing provincial public bonds, reduce interest rates, and extend the repayment period to ease the debt burden. The Hangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Banking and Financial Industry Association believe that this move affects the interests of merchants themselves and have submitted petitions to the provincial government requesting that the original plan not be changed and that the bonds be maintained. The banking and financial industries also convened a joint meeting and resolved to send a telegram to the central government's various departments and the Zhejiang Provincial Government to maintain credit and contracts. The original telegram stated: "An investigation reveals that Zhejiang Province has issued seven types of bonds: bonds for repaying old debts, highway bonds, construction bonds, disaster relief bonds, clearing old debts, provincial treasury bills, and local bonds. The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance has borrowed more than 11 million yuan from the banking and financial industries. Recently, it has been rumored that the Department of Finance intends to reduce interest rates and extend the principal repayment periods for various bonds and change the contracts for various loans. Public sentiment is anxious and unsettled. If this is not just a rumor and actually comes to pass, the social economy will be disrupted and panic will arise. The Association, being responsible for Zhejiang's finances, and considering the current market downturn, must present the situation that Zhejiang's bonds cannot be reorganized and various loans cannot have their contracts changed.

Regarding public bonds, the current Zhejiang provincial bonds are divided into three categories: The first is the reorganization case, which includes the repayment of highway construction, revitalization, and clearing of public bonds. The second is the provincial treasury case, the twenty-first Zhejiang provincial treasury bills. The third is the local bond case, the twenty-third Zhejiang provincial local bonds. The issuance of all bonds, whether solicited from the public based on the face value of the bond, or mortgaged against debts owed to the banking and financial industries, all designate provincial tax revenue as the fund. The bond fund listed in the provincial budget for the twentieth year was 8,001,400 yuan. Even with the shortfall in tax revenue and the expenditure of collection fees, it is more than sufficient to pay the principal and interest on the various bonds in the twenty-fourth year, which amounted to 5,428,600 yuan, and therefore cannot be reorganized.

Regarding loans, the Department of Finance has borrowed from the banking and financial industries in Shanghai, Hangzhou, and other places over the years. As of November 11th of the twenty-fourth year, the total outstanding amount was 11,125,399 yuan, 5 jiao, 6 fen, 1 li, with various bonds as collateral for more than nine-tenths of the total amount. Investigations show that some loans have been partially repaid, while others have not been repaid at all, but all have contractual relationships. According to legal principles, no party may arbitrarily change them. Even early repayment requires the consent of the lender. If the government does not understand the difficulties of merchants and takes extraordinary measures, the capital on which finance relies for circulation will inevitably be severely damaged. The impact on operators is small, but the hindrance to the social credit system is great. The banking and financial industries, in order to maintain the normal interlocking relationship between finance and finance, absolutely cannot accept any plans to change the original plan. We should respectfully consider the capital of the bondholders and the credit of the contracts, fulfill the sincerity of the original plan, make a clear announcement, so as to dispel public doubts and show great faith. However, regarding this case, the Director of Finance, Cheng Yuanfan, has twice gone to Beijing to consult with the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Finance. As soon as there are concrete results from the discussion, the reorganization plan can be announced and implemented. It is said that reorganizing Zhejiang's debt is a necessary fact for the finances. Both the central and local authorities have long had this intention, so this case is inevitable. The opposition from the banking and financial industries may not be effective. (March 12th)

Guangdong Province Actively Consolidates the Defense of the Eastern Border of Chaozhou and Meizhou 84

Shantou Dispatch: The counties of Chaozhou and Meizhou in the eastern Guangdong region are adjacent to the border of Fujian and are an important area for national and provincial defense. The Guangdong authorities have repeatedly received information from various sources that the leaders of the civilian army along the coastal areas of Zhangzhou and Quanzhou in southern Fujian have recently received support and guidance from a certain party, forming a "Great Alliance," advocating "Fujian Autonomy," and that a pseudo-autonomous government and autonomous army are already brewing. Commander-in-Chief Chen of the Guangdong Army specially summoned the military officers stationed in the eastern region, Li Yangjing, Li Hanhun, Huang Yanzhen, and others, to a meeting at his private residence in Meiyuan Village on the 5th to discuss suppressing bandits and consolidating the eastern border. Jiang Dingwen, the Pacification Director of Fujian Province, expressed concern about the security of Zhangzhou and Quanzhou. It is reported that on the 7th of this month, he cracked down on secret organizations of traitors in Zhangzhou and Xiamen. In addition to reporting to the highest officials to quickly determine a national defense strategy, he also informed the authorities and ordered the garrison in Chaoshan to take strict precautions. Huang Renhuan, the commander of the Independent First Division, gave a speech to the military officers in Jiaoling on the 7th, stating that, according to the order of the headquarters, all officers and soldiers, whether at the front or in the rear, are not allowed to take leave at this time. Those who have already taken leave must return to their posts within five days from the date of the announcement in order to maintain their duties. The border defense of Chaozhou, Meizhou, Fujian, and Jiangxi has become tense in recent days.

Major General Hirata, a military attaché from Japan, and Commander Hosogaya of the Fifth Torpedo Squadron arrived in Shantou aboard the flagship "Yubari" on the 3rd and were warmly welcomed by the Japanese consul and the chairman of the residents' association. It is said that Hirata's visit to the south is to comfort Japanese warships stationed at ports in southern China and to inspect Japanese and Taiwanese residents, but the content is not so simple. On the 4th, two military attachés from Japan stationed in Guangdong, Major Taihei Hideo and Captain Ogawa Kanji, arrived in Shantou via the Dongjiang First Trunk Line. A platoon leader of the Guangdong Chen's constabulary led twelve constables to escort them along the way. After the two military attachés arrived in Shantou on the 4th, Japanese consul's office, naval, and army officers had a very important meeting. The content is not known to outsiders. On the same day, Hirata, Hosogaya, and the captains of the "Asagao" and "Fuyou," both anchored in Shantou, attended the meeting. After the meeting, at 2 p.m., the captains of the "Fuyou" and "Asagao," accompanied by Oburo, a clerk from the Japanese consulate, went to the Public Security Bureau to see Song Dejian, the Director of the bureau. They had a secret conversation in the Director's office for two hours. It is said that the conversation was about the death of patrolman Kakuda Susumu on the 21st of last month. The Japanese side, under the pretext of protecting its residents, demanded to increase the number of Japanese consulate police to assist the Shantou Public Security Bureau in maintaining public order. The outcome is not known to the outside world. On the 5th, Hirata, Hosogaya, Taihei, Ogawa, the Japanese Consul Harada, and 18 key members from the "Yubari," "Fuyou," and "Asagao" and the army and navy, were led by Huang Muyi (a Taiwanese), the financial backer of the Xinghua Foreign Firm on Yushan Street, to visit Chaoan City. They left in the morning and returned in the evening. All famous scenic spots inside and outside Chaoan, as well as important transportation hubs on the roads and waterways, were thoroughly surveyed. On the evening of the 5th, Hirata and others took the "Yubari" to Xiamen, while Taihei and Ogawa remained in Shantou, residing in the Huashang Hotel in Tongyi West Lane. Those who frequent this hotel are leaders of a certain province from Fuzhou, Xiamen, and Shantou, and are closely watched by Chaozhou, Shantou, and military and police authorities. A certain leader who came to Shantou from Taiwan, Fuzhou, and Xiamen hosted a banquet for Taihei and others, which often lasted all night. The extent of their busyness can be imagined. On the 6th, Taihei claimed that he wanted to travel to Fengshun and Meizhou, and return to the province via the upper reaches of the Dongjiang River. Liang Shiying, the platoon leader of the constabulary who escorted them to Shantou, dissuaded him. On the 7th, Taihei and others again wanted to take a bus to Chenghai Xiaoping Huanggang, and go to Xiamen via Zhao'an, notifying the municipal government to transfer to the East District Office to protect their travels in various places, but they were persuaded by the mayor to give up. The Japanese military officials are touring the interior during this freezing weather and drizzle, their interest is not superficial. The reader can understand their intentions.

The Case of Zhang Wei: Murderer Chen Juncen Commits Suicide in Prison - Han Fuqu Cables Report to the Central Government - 85

Jinan Dispatch: On January 2nd of last year, the Provincial New Life Movement Promotion Association convened a lantern festival, using the New Year opportunity to conduct expanded publicity. That evening, at the Jinde Hall, amidst the bright lights and bustling crowds, Zhang Weicun, a Central Committee member, Standing Committee member of the Shandong Provincial Party Headquarters, and member of the Shandong Provincial Government, was shot and killed. At the time, military police thoroughly searched the Jinde Hall but found nothing. Subsequently, the provincial government offered a reward for the capture of the murderer. Finally, on the 4th of that month, the murderer, Chen Juncen, was apprehended. Chen was the director of the Special Affairs Office of the Provincial Party Headquarters (i.e., the anti-communist squad leader). The firearms, bullets, and circumstances before and after the incident provided irrefutable evidence, and Chen also confessed. He was detained in a well-appointed room within the prisoner holding area. The details of the case were recorded in the newspapers at the time. Now, more than a year has passed, and the prisoner lived freely. Unexpectedly, at one o'clock in the morning on the 10th, he used his belt to hang himself. Because it was late at night, by the time he was discovered, it was too late to save him, and he died. The military judge stationed at the prisoner holding area, Lu Angbin, reported the incident. Subsequently, the Third Route Army Headquarters dispatched military judge Yuan Daotian, along with Chen Qinglan, a forensic examiner from the Jinan District Court, to the scene to conduct a detailed examination. The deceased was 37 years old, originally from Anhua County, Hunan Province. It was confirmed that he had died by hanging, with a cloth belt mark around his throat. There were no other injuries. An autopsy report was completed, and a coffin was prepared to enshroud the body, which was temporarily placed in the City God Temple, awaiting family members to claim it for burial. Chairman Han has already telegraphed the situation of the prisoner's suicide to President Jiang of the Central Executive Yuan for review.

New Commissioner Assumes Office: Zhu Jiwu, the newly appointed special commissioner for opium cases in this county, arrived in Songjiang on the 12th and went to the county government to assume his duties.

Songjiang

On the 13th, during the trial of an opium case, the police were first ordered to bring Qian Jide, a private opium smoker held in custody, to court. Because he was seriously ill, a request was made to release him on bail. When being brought from the prison and passing in front of the County Court, he collapsed and died. The incident was immediately reported to the county government. After reviewing the records, it was found that the opium addict was from Jinshanwei. He was arrested and imprisoned in November of last year. He became seriously ill in prison, and his brother offered bail, which was approved for him to be summoned and released, but he unfortunately died halfway.

Yangzhou Postman Runs Away with Large Sum of Money

The postal service in Touqiao Town, Third District of Jiangdu, was originally handled by Jiao Yuantai General Store. Last spring, it was converted into a third-class post office. Because Jiao Bingchun, the owner of Jiao Yuantai, had been handling the business for many years and had made achievements, his son, Ming-san, was recommended for the examination and passed. He was assigned to the Laoyao area as a postman. A Mr. Lu from Nanjing provided a written guarantee of 200 yuan. However, Jiao Mingsan absconded with 1,000 yuan from the post office. Trial of Murder Case of Yu Dong Woman Concludes in Nantong

Seeing bloodstains on the bedding, he became suspicious and reported the incident to the authorities. The prosecutor detained the two suspects and interrogated them, and the body was exhumed. They confessed to the crime and were prosecuted with the death penalty. Yesterday, Judge Hong of the Criminal Court conducted a trial. Gu Wang and Gu Haitao both retracted their confessions, but the evidence was conclusive. The trial concluded, and the verdict is scheduled to be announced on the 18th.

Central Bank to Collect Old Mixed-Color Subsidiary Coins 86

After the Central Mint cast subsidiary coins upon the order of the Ministry of Finance, which the Central Bank has exclusively issued and circulated in the market, it has been decided to find a way to collect the old mixed-color subsidiary coins. Xi Demao, Director of the Business Bureau of the Central Bank, has already met with Wei Jingzhou, Deputy Director of the Central Mint, and the British-owned Tram Company, the British-owned China Motor Bus Company, and the French-owned Water and Electricity Company to discuss the matter. The copper coins received from daily ticket sales by trams and buses will be collected by the Central Bank at the price stipulated by the Ministry of Finance: 300 copper coins for 1 yuan in legal tender. The total amount collected each month will be 240,000 yuan in legal tender. After implementation, due to issues such as transportation and storage, David, the manager of Sassoon Banking Corporation, raised the issue for discussion at the regular meeting of the Central Mint Audit Committee yesterday. It was decided to hand it over to member Xi Demao, together with Wei Jingzhou, Deputy Director of the Central Mint, and senior personnel from the tram and bus companies, to negotiate a proper solution on the 16th (Monday). It is reported that in addition to stacking the collected copper coins in the Central Mint and Central Bank warehouses, the Central Bank will temporarily store them in the warehouses of the tram and bus companies. However, the legal tender due for collection will be paid monthly.

New Subsidiary Coins Cast in February Approved for Release. The Joint Bank Reserves Committee resolved yesterday at a meeting.

Zhu Boquan first reported on the preparations. Because the funds have been fully subscribed, it was decided to open on Monday, March 16th. The meeting adjourned at approximately 4 PM. It is reported that since the acceptance house is the first of its kind, it has been decided to conduct a trial run first. If successful, it will be expanded.

National Federation of Commerce Receives Reply from the Ministry of Finance Yesterday 92

Rules for Silver Management

Continue to process in accordance with previous instructions. The National Federation of Commerce, at the request of representatives of the silver industry, telegraphed the Ministry of Finance on the second of this month to request approval to amend the rules for silver management. The Federation received a reply from the Ministry of Finance yesterday, Qian Zi No. 8849, stating, "Your telegram dated the winter of March 25th regarding the request of representatives of the national silver industry, Ran Xizhang, and others to amend the rules for silver management has been received. This case has already been submitted directly by the representatives and a request has been made to the Ministry. The Ministry believes that the rules for silver management promulgated by the Ministry are intended to control the use of silver, reduce the raw material costs of silver products, and promote the improvement of manual techniques. While implementing the government's consolidation policies, there is still an intention to safeguard the industry. As for the rule that the addition of pure silver must not exceed 30%, after detailed research, the Ministry ordered the Central Mint to allocate and use materials containing more alloy components, which does not hinder manual techniques. The previous instructions of the Ministry should still be followed and purchased faithfully." You are hereby notified.

We believe that telephones, as a corporate enterprise and a tool for communication, should share weal and woe with users, striving for widespread impact. However, commercial companies are not considering this, but instead use their exclusive operating contract as a shield, engaging in exploitation and restricting commerce and hindering transportation, which is incomprehensible. We have read in the newspaper that Executive Committee members of your association, such as Xie Xiaochu, have jointly proposed convening a representative meeting to discuss and resolve the telephone fee issue. At the same time, we received a letter from the brothel industry in the foreign concession, requesting assistance. After submitting it to the 15th Executive Committee for discussion, it was concluded that the decision by the Shanghai Municipal Council to approve the Shanghai Telephone Company's price increase was a serious violation of public opinion, and the attending Chinese directors abandoned their position as representatives of the ratepayers, which is also inappropriate. However, since this measure has already been implemented, if relief is not promptly sought, the future will be even more dire. Your esteemed association is the general organization for Chinese ratepayers in the settlement. If this issue is not vigorously contested, it will be difficult to dispel external doubts. Now that the situation is such, and your Executive Committee members have also spoken out righteously, advocating for submission to the ratepayers' meeting for resolution, our association believes that this view is deeply in line with the consensus of ratepayers. Therefore, we are specially conveying this decision by letter, urging you to promptly convene a ratepayers' meeting to seek thorough relief. If this is still ignored, it will disappoint the expectations of the ratepayers. We are sending this letter specifically in the hope that you will investigate and respond accordingly."

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Submits a Request for Correction Regarding the Illegal Procedure of the Finance Bureau Detaining People for Tax Arrears; the Illegal Usual Procedure Should Be Revoked and Abolished 99

The Shanghai Timber Industry Association submitted a request to the Municipal Party Headquarters for protection regarding the detention of Chen Qizhang, manager of the Futai Timber Company, by the Zhabei Collection Office of the Municipal Finance Bureau. The submission was published in this newspaper on the 12th of this month. According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce also submitted a request to the municipal government yesterday, following the letter from the Timber Industry Association on the 11th of this month. Except for the original letter, which is omitted here, the letter stated: "The main point of this case is that the Municipal North Collection Office, in pursuing tax arrears, should not have detained Chen Qizhang, manager of the Futai Timber Company, for 28 hours, taking fingerprints and photos, as if he were a major thief, until the industry jointly provided a guarantee before releasing him. Tax arrears are only a financial matter. Since the company has assets available for execution, there is no reason to restrict the person's personal freedom. Even in terms of court enforcement of debts, it is not customary to detain a person if there are assets available for compulsory execution. Even according to Article 6, Paragraph 1 of the Administrative Enforcement Law, there is a similar restriction. This case does not apply to direct compulsory measures against a person. The collection office's practice of detaining people as a usual procedure for dealing with tax resistance is an illegal order, whether it was created by the collection office itself or approved by the bureau. The responsible officials should be subject to penalties for violations, and the long-standing illegal usual procedure should be revoked and abolished by the supervisory authority, with a strict order not to be used in the future. It is appropriate to submit this document to your government for review and approval for implementation, as it is in the public interest."
