Women's Special

Written After Women's Day 196

— Wei Jing

"March 8th" is International Women's Day. It is a memorial day for women to break free from shackles and strive for independent personalities. Naturally, the women's liberation movement is still only slowly progressing on a long and rugged road, far from its destination, and even more so in our Chinese women's community, which has the longest history of being shackled, the women's liberation movement seems even more naive. Therefore, this "March 8th" is undoubtedly only the first small firecracker of a women's movement, emitting a faint spark.

Although "March 8th" is only a small spark, it contains two great meanings: First, obtaining liberation from shackles; second, obtaining equal status after being liberated.

In China, "women's liberation" has obviously been developing in a localized and deformed way in recent years, seemingly limited to the student circles of a few major cities. In the student circles of major cities, at the very least, there is the freedom to criticize all unreasonable oppression of women. However, undoubtedly, once one steps out of school, or during vacations when returning to family, a large part will involuntarily make efforts for the liberation movement in a considerably unfree way. Because the environment of society and family still possesses strong barriers that women with considerable education cannot destroy, and everywhere there are traps and shackles that imprison women, opening their mouths, ready to swallow women - regardless of whether they are unliberated or liberated women.

Even a few liberated women, stepping into society and demanding a refuge after liberation with men standing on an equal footing, still show a situation of blurred vision. All that can be seen is a terrifying shadow. Regarding this level, we naturally cannot but attribute it to history, because our society is a society in which men have devoured women for thousands of years. However, men devouring women is an established historical fact, and the psychological construction required by the women's movement is precisely the effort to overthrow this established fact. However, the women's movement in the past, up to now, has obviously only focused on the incomplete and ununiversal liberation of women. As for what to do after the liberation that is better than nothing, has a considerable position been constructed to accommodate the rare liberated women? No one has bothered to ask. Therefore, the majority of the few liberated women, struggling out of old shackles, unknowingly fall into new traps. Although this is a social disadvantage, in fact, the short-sighted policy of the women's liberation movement cannot but be held responsible.

The author has a female cousin who fought for the right to receive higher education from stubborn parents and from the environment where "lack of talent is a virtue in women." During her school years, she also fought for the right to marital autonomy, and broke off the marriage with her incompetent fiancé, who was engaged to her by her parents at the age of thirteen. Although this caused a serious conflict with her family and suffered the pain of severe sanctions from the old society, she was able to fight with tenacious courage. However, after a short period of time, she had no choice but to serve the society due to the severance of family economic relations. Who knew that she was actually raped and became a concubine the year before last. By the time the secret was revealed, she was involved in a lawsuit in court, and after escaping the relationship, she had already become a woman rejected by her parents and clan. At present, although she is continuing her studies with a little alimony from her divorce, her future, naturally, still cannot find optimistic light.

Naturally, it is just one example. In recent years, I don't know how many similar events have occurred in the process of the women's movement, so I hope that everyone will commemorate "March 8th," recognizing the first important meaning, and must pay more attention to the second important meaning. Otherwise, "the women's movement" in China will suffer an unexpected failure and lead to a complete loss of effort.

Respect Your Wife, Cherish Your Children 197

— Translated by Chen Xuezhao

The elimination of the bourgeoisie in our country has brought about the elimination of bourgeois marriage forms.

However, it would be too false to say that everything is perfect in our family relationships, and that all relationships between families and between single men and women are peaceful. The truth is not so. We have given women all kinds of rights, we have opened up a path for them to work and live independently, but we have not yet removed the remaining oppression of capitalist society. This hateful oppression is always felt in family relationships in the Soviet state.

One example of these bourgeois remnants is the irresponsible and inconsiderate attitude of some individuals towards their family obligations.

The morally unstable elements in the people believe that the greatest freedom given by the October Revolution to men and women is the right to do immoral things in family life. Although such elements constitute only a small part of our population, their number is still too large because their wrongdoings go unpunished.

Conscious proletarians show respect for their families and their obligations, whether to their wives or parents. Only bourgeois priests and spoiled sons, who know they are bad elements in the family, still maintain their old habits. To say that thinking of family is a petty-bourgeois idea is only true for hypocritical bourgeois loafers.

Being a good member of a family is fulfilling a responsibility that we should fulfill. A bad member of a family will not be a good Soviet citizen, nor will they be a good worker in a social plan.

Although in our country, women have legal equality and economic independence, they are still the weaker part until society can fully educate all children: we should protect them because most of the people who neglect family responsibilities are always men.

In our country, no one has to be forced to continue their married life. We do not have ugly divorce cases. But the right to divorce given by Soviet law is not a right to immorality. Our laws assume that men and women know their responsibilities. But the responsibility of men is greater. A family without children loses its meaning, and the education of children requires a lot of work and attention. This work should be the joint responsibility of parents, and the law on child support should be strictly enforced. A father who abandons his wife and children and feels as free as a bird is a criminal. Courts that are tolerant of these fathers who only want to escape their responsibilities are also committing crimes.

Socialism wants to extend its protection to everyone so that the population can increase. Our youth are the healthiest in the world, both physically and mentally. Their character has gradually been shaped in the constant struggle for socialism and has been re-educated according to the ideas of evolution. This kind of thinking is not related to excessive lust or contempt for women. Bourgeois remnants will be completely eradicated.

This is the difference in our system: it is the glory of the Soviet people to educate their children and respect their wives and mothers.

Recently, some people in our country have advocated for new virtuous mothers and good wives. Virtuous mothers and good wives are certainly what we need, but it is still useless to have virtuous mothers and good wives without virtuous husbands and good fathers. I felt that this short article in the Russian newspaper strongly advocating for virtuous husbands and good fathers was meaningful, so I translated it. — Translator.

Nursery

Understanding Prenatal Education 198

— Jiu Yong

Nowadays, some educators advocate for total human education, including prenatal education in addition to family education, school education, and social education, and they believe it is very important. This may be based on the development of human beings: when a fetus is in the mother's womb, it obtains nutrition and protection from the mother's body, and the mother's body and mind are sufficient to affect the fetus. Prenatal education is established under this "hypothesis," and all countries in the East and West acknowledge this.

In our country, Zhu Xi also described in his "Elementary Learning": "The Biography of Women says: 'In ancient times, when a woman was pregnant, she would not lie on her side, sit on the edge, or stand askew; she would not eat strange tastes, would not eat meat that was not properly cut, would not sit on a mat that was not properly placed, would not look at obscene colors, would not listen to lewd sounds; at night, she would have a blind musician recite poems and talk about proper matters. In this way, the child born would have a proper appearance and be exceptionally talented.'" This illustrates that the mother should pay attention to the norms of daily life during pregnancy.

Even in our folk customs, there are similar legends and stories, but they are tinged with excessive superstition.

As for the educational value of prenatal education, we do not ask about its effects, but a mother who pays such attention to the fetus is truly educating her son. From an educational point of view, the influence of the mother's education that we expect is actually greater than the value of prenatal education itself. From a scientific point of view, we use today's scientific knowledge to explain:

Chronic and acute diseases of the mother's body are harmful to the fetus.

Prolonged worries, emotional depression, laziness, and overwork of the mother's body are harmful to the mother's nutrition and directly harmful to the fetus's physical development.

The mother's intake of poisons and toxic substances can damage reproductive cells and affect the fetus's body and mind.

Syphilis transmitted in utero can also harm the development of the fetus.

From this, we can imagine what kind of health care the mother needs during pregnancy. Zhu Xi's description is indeed very consistent with scientific views.

However, medical scholars do not recognize these, except for the mechanisms that can affect the fetus's body, the relationship between the mother's body and the fetus is only that the mother's body provides blood to the fetus. Although nutritional disorders, poisoning, and diseases of the mother's body are transmitted to the fetus through the blood, these adverse effects are not detected. They believe that rather than fearing mothers who do not pay attention to prenatal education, it is better to pay attention to spiritual education after birth.

In our understanding, future prenatal education should be based on genetic instructions and the lessons of eugenics, pay attention to the conditions of ideal partners, and pay attention to hygiene during pregnancy, in order to produce babies with excellent qualities.

Standard Woman

A Record of Madam Huang Keqiang 199

— Lin Qian

Revolutionary martyr Huang Keqiang has made great contributions in the glorious history of our nation's revolution. His wife, Ms. Xu Zonghan, is also a heroine among women. After Huang's death, she resolutely continued her husband's aspirations, constantly fighting against the evil forces of the Northern Government. Being eager for public good and righteousness seems to be her innate character. Whenever there is a national salvation movement, she always helps with all her might. I remember during the May Fourth Movement in the eighth year of the Republic of China, student associations were established in various places. She then organized the Women's Federation in Shanghai, and from the Women's Federation, she took the lead in organizing the National Federation of All Circles. It was truly a call from the heights, and all the mountains responded. Industrial, commercial, academic, and other groups from various provinces and regions sent representatives to participate. At that time, to arouse the public and lead to such a phenomenon of popular enthusiasm, she naturally had a considerable contribution. Moreover, when the Shanghai people fought against the warlords, she always served as the vanguard, often leading female comrades to rush into the ranks of the military police. The military police were instead pushed back by them, and the male comrades often gained safety because of this. Since the Revolutionary Army established its capital in Nanjing, she saw that the revolution had been successful, but she still did not want to enjoy a comfortable life, so she founded the Poor Children's Training Institute, specializing in educating and raising general impoverished children. Over the years, she has cultivated no less than a thousand people. The facilities in the institute are very complete, and the main courses are about teaching industrial and vocational skills, such as wireless telegraphy, typing, sewing, weaving towels and socks, and various rattan products, so that students can make a living after graduation. The students who graduate each year should naturally leave the institute according to the regulations, but because the students do not have the ability to be economically independent, many still refuse to leave the institute. She understands the students' difficulties, so she does her best to find a way out for them, recommending them to various public and private factories. However, as time goes by and the number of people increases, recommendations also gradually become difficult, so graduation season becomes her major hurdle. For the sake of the graduates' future, she is often so tired that she forgets to eat and sleep. From this, one can see her painstaking efforts to serve the public. If the wives of all the great men in the country were like this Madam Huang, not only would the poor children of the whole country be saved, but China would have been saved long ago.

Cooking Knowledge 200

Vegetarian Ham: Everyone knows that ham is made from pork legs, so how can it be vegetarian? But the vegetarian ham I am talking about is made from tofu skin. First, soak ten or twenty sheets of tofu skin in good soy sauce, add dried shrimp, large ones soak for an hour, then take them out, stack them one by one, and mix the dried shrimp and soy sauce into the skin, then roll them up, into a long strip the size of a silver dollar, then wrap it in a clean cloth, and tie it tightly with rope on the outside. After it is tied, put it in a coarse bowl and steam it over water. Steam the large ones for two hours, then take them out and cut them into pieces the size and thickness of silver dollars. It is very delicious. If you eat it with porridge, it is very suitable.

Sugar Sweet Potato: Use native sweet potato (red skin and red heart, if there is no native sweet potato, you can also use foreign sweet potato). Remove the skin, cut it into round pieces, and fry it in soybean oil until it turns yellow (you must fry them one by one to fry them thoroughly). Then add water, white sugar, and lard and cook them together for one or two hours, then they will be cooked until soft. It is sweet and delicious to eat and is a good afternoon snack.

Pork Floss: Use several pounds of pork, remove the skin and fat, leaving only the lean meat (i.e., lean meat), wash it clean, add soy sauce, wine, green onions, ginger, etc., and braise it according to the method of braising pork. Then use chopsticks to break the meat into shreds, then cook it again. When the soup is about to dry, stir it with chopsticks again. When the soup is cooked dry, add sesame oil and stir-fry with a shovel for about one or two hours, then you can stir-fry it until crispy. Take it out of the pot at any time and put it in a ceramic jar. However, the jar lid must be covered after the pork floss has cooled completely, otherwise it will easily become soft and not crispy. (Lean Qiu)

Snake (4) 201

— Qin Wang Yin Jiu

After exchanging a few pleasantries, they soon arrived at Deyue Lou, and picked a table upstairs to sit down.

"Your little official must have been quite frightened that day? I happened to see it with my own eyes!" After drinking a cup of tea, Wu Er first mentioned the main topic. Without Yu Zhongqing questioning him, he described as much as possible the situation of how everyone brought a red-banded snake to scare the little mute: he just moved himself from an active position to a bystander's position.

"So that's how it is! Yu Zhongqing sighed, seemingly very sad, after listening.

"Mr. Yu, what's strange is indeed very strange," The two walnuts in Wu Er's hands were still clattering. "Your little official was never known to be timid. I never saw him afraid of anything. In terms of strength, I, Wu Er, admire him even more. But I don't understand why he's so... so afraid of snakes?"

Yu Zhongqing did not answer immediately. He first looked at Wu Er's eager face with a pair of bright, spirited eyes, at which time he already understood the intention of this busybody who had specially invited him to tea, but he was also unwilling to disappoint Wu Er, and finally told the truth.

"Brother Wu Er, you see that I am now a peaceful farmer," Yu Zhongqing shook the blue cloth short jacket he was wearing. "But I used to be a heartless military officer, you may also know. And before that? Our family were all hunters. Decades ago, in Hunan, our Yu family in Xiangyin was quite well-known. It's not that I'm bragging, but no matter how ferocious a beast was, it wouldn't think about going back if it ran into us. But it's sad to say: my grandfather and father hunted tigers, leopards, wolves and so on all their lives, and never missed a shot, but in the end they both died from snake venom... One died with his whole body festering, and the other was swollen bigger than an ox, almost unable to fit into a coffin..."

A look of anger and fear gradually welled up on Yu Zhongqing's face, which made Wu Er feel a little hair-raising.

"Before their death, they both said that snakes were the most sinister things, and even the greatest heroes should still avoid them if they see them. From then on, the people in our family warned each other to run away when they saw a snake. But my second brother didn't believe it. His kung fu was also the best, and he was determined to avenge his father and grandfather. Once he saw a snake, he had to chop it to death before he would stop. It turned out that one time he chopped a small green snake less than three feet long into three pieces. Seeing that it was dead, he was too lazy to bury it. The next day, when he walked by, he saw that only the middle and end sections were left. He looked for a long time, but still couldn't find the head section. Just as he was about to walk back, he suddenly felt something wiggling in his crotch. He hurriedly pulled off his pants, but it was too late. That section of the snake's head had desperately drilled into his anus, so of course it was over!"

Wu Er listened with a mix of fear and fascination, and unconsciously stared blankly at Yu Zhongqing's bitter smile.

"At that time, my child was only four years old, but he already understood things. Seeing his uncle rolling on the ground for two days and two nights before dying, he was scared to death. After that, as long as we mentioned the word 'snake,' he would be scared and cry." Yu Zhongqing sighed again when he said this: "So today, I sincerely thank you, Brother Wu Er, for asking about this matter, and I will honestly tell you, and by the way, I beg you to say hello to all the neighbors and don't joke with my little mute again! I am truly grateful!"

Wu Er couldn't help but hit his own leg twice to express his deep regret. When he looked at Jin Zhongqing again, his eyes were already completely red. (End)

Special Report from This Newspaper

A Ten-Minute Meeting with Madam Mei Huaquan 202

— Ji Ping

Chinese women are not incompetent, but it is a pity that few are aware. To fight for equal rights between men and women, one must first develop one's own strength. To adapt to the trends of the times, one must encourage learning and cultivate morality.

Madam Mei Huaquan is a pioneer in advocating for the women's movement and is enthusiastic about social undertakings. The women's circles in Shanghai all recognize her as a leader. I have also admired her name for a long time, so I decided to visit her, hoping to report her twenty years of experience in presiding over the women's movement to the general women, so that everyone can get a correct concept. Although our conversation was only ten minutes, her very sincere and thorough words can be considered to be pertinent.

Madam Mei is originally from Guangdong and was born in Hong Kong. When she was six or seven years old, she followed her kind mother to visit Penang and Xiangshan, where she lived for ten years before studying at Columbia University in the United States, studying education. She was a classmate of Mr. Mei. After returning to China and getting married, she has lived in Shanghai for more than twenty years. She said that the reason why she is willing to serve society is because she received all kinds of stimulation overseas when she was young and felt that a woman must work hard in society. Like Hawaii and the United States, there are traces of our overseas Chinese everywhere. Regardless of whether they are men or women, they have always been discriminated against unequally by foreigners. The weakness of national power is certainly a major reason, but the low level of knowledge of overseas Chinese is also closely related. I am a woman, a knowledgeable woman, how can I improve the ability of my female compatriots? To win an equal position internationally? That was my established ambition. In those days, the wives of our country's ambassadors and consuls abroad were also old-fashioned in their thinking and did not know international etiquette, so there were many disadvantages in the international position. Foreigners ridiculed us Chinese as not an excellent nation. Do you think you can stand the injustice? Later, when I arrived in Shanghai, I decided to fight for the status of my female compatriots and change the international attitude of contempt for my female compatriots.

At that time, there were hardly any women's organizations in Shanghai, so we contacted the pioneers of the women's circles, gathered our strength, organized together, and worked together for society. First, we established the National Association of Young Women's Christian Associations as a vanguard team to promote women's sports, study women's health, and handle women's supplementary education; to improve the efficiency of women's intellectual, moral, and physical education. Fortunately, with the help of all walks of life, there has been considerable success in recent years. I have worked in this association for twenty years and have been the president for seven years, and I have put in a lot of energy. In addition, the International Council of Women and the Chinese Women's Association are also two major organizations that I serve. Today, international women in Shanghai not only feel that Chinese women are not incompetent, but also believe that the spirit of service of Chinese women may be stronger than theirs. It is a pity that there are still too few comrades, and we have not reached the entire female masses.

According to her twenty years of experience in guiding the women's movement, she feels that the intelligence of Chinese women is not lower than that of Western women, but their physical strength is slightly inferior. She deeply feels that most women in the upper class lack social thought and national concepts. They only care about their own enjoyment and waste their precious time in improper entertainment. If they spend a little more time, put in a little more effort, and donate a little more money, to think about the poor masses and seek the interests of women themselves, then social reform will definitely be hopeful. Although the economic situation of women in middle-class families is slightly worse, they can set aside time and energy to contribute to society. They must first train their own abilities, develop their personal ambitions, and strive to understand everything that is unclear, be diligent in learning, and not bury their own ambitions solely for the sake of the family. As for poor women, it is really pitiful to say, they work hard all year round and cannot get enough food and clothing. Although we have the grand wish to provide relief, it is difficult to popularize a drop in the bucket. This is a problem of the entire political, economic, and social system, and it is not easy to improve without the power of the state. She also said that Shanghai is such a big city, and the Young Women's Christian Association still rents other people's houses, has no land, and has no funds, not to mention not being as good as foreign countries, but also not as good as the Young Women's Christian Associations in Guangdong, Hong Kong, and Beijing. In this regard, she deeply regrets the cold attitude of most women in Shanghai towards social undertakings!

Madam Mei also talked about her own family. She said that we are an organization of a new family. There are no elders above, and everything is decided by my husband and I. Now there are two children, one male and one female, who are both in school. Family life takes a simple and economical approach. I have always taken care of household affairs in the morning, and worked for the above three women's organizations in the afternoon. In recent years, the affairs of the association have become more developed than before, so daily matters can be considered trivial, but I am very interested in this and do not feel tired at all. Finally, I asked her what Chinese women should do to meet the needs of modern times? She thought for a while and said very calmly: "The so-called era and the so-called trend are constantly changing, but for us women, regardless of how it changes, it is most important to diligently seek knowledge and cultivate morality. With knowledge and morality, we can adapt to the needs of the times. Women should contribute their surplus energy to society in addition to fulfilling their duties. Some people raise their hands and shout for equal rights between men and women, but they only enjoy themselves. I do not approve of this..."

I only talked to her for ten minutes, but her calmness and sincerity left a very deep impression.

A Shortcut to Treating Acne and Freckles 216

— (Jingcheng)

The cause of acne is the excessive accumulation of sebum in the sebaceous glands or the blockage of the sebaceous gland openings. During puberty, our sebaceous glands secrete more sebum, or obstructions such as hair follicle parasites and dirt block the sebaceous excretory ducts, hindering sebum excretion, thus causing this condition. Therefore, acne is common in young people. The symptoms are small papules protruding from the sebaceous gland openings, like sesame seeds, with black or purple tips. If pressed with a fingernail, there is a rice-like fatty nodule inside. The locations where this condition occurs are the forehead, nose, and cheeks, but it can also occur on the chest and back, although this is rare. Freckles are named freckles because their spots resemble the spots on a sparrow's feathers. They can occur on all parts of the body, but they are most often seen on the face. They are almost indistinguishable from summer spots. Summer spots appear in summer and disappear in winter, while freckles remain all year round. They often appear in childhood and become more prominent during puberty. The cause is a congenital change in skin quality. Since acne and freckles are the most common facial skin disorders for us, methods for treating these two conditions are also the most needed for us. In view of this, Shanghai Tongren Western Drug Company has invented a kind of "Mianli" cream, which specializes in treating acne and freckles, and has remarkable results. Since its sales, it has spread throughout the country, which is enough to be a shortcut for the treatment of those suffering from freckles and acne.

Psoriasis 218

— (Zhu Qiuyuan)

Psoriasis, also known as scaly ringworm, is a skin disease caused by nerve and blood vessel disorders. Its nature is extremely stubborn, often lasting for more than ten years. At first, the skin develops rash-like spots or small nodules, forming irregular circles, dark red in color. After a period of time, the surface is covered with silvery-white scales. If the scales are removed, blood stains are visible. Later, the surrounding area gradually expands, winding into a map-like shape, while the center gradually fades. If left untreated for a long time, it spreads widely, often from head to toe, and the skin becomes red and covered with layers of scales. Psoriasis occurs on the neck, palms, soles, and extensor surfaces of the elbow and knee joints, often causing severe itching. Treatment methods include medication, radium therapy, or X-ray irradiation. For medication treatment, "Ganlu" from Tongren Western Drug Company is the best. "Ganlu" uses the correct medications and is legally formulated. Each bottle sells for 1 yuan.

Selling Books to Seek Education 227

— Zhou Ge

The article titled "Pleading for a Child: Selling Books to Seek Education," published in the local supplement of the Shen Bao on March 9th, goes something like this: A young man studying at a certain middle school is about to graduate this semester. However, due to poverty, and with graduation being a critical juncture, his father, despite piecing together twenty old silver dollars with great difficulty, is still ten dollars short and at a loss. He has no choice but to sell the one hundred and fifty-plus volumes of the "Children's Library" that he has at home, reducing the price from the original eighteen dollars to ten dollars in order to make up for the shortfall in tuition.

The current society is one that emphasizes "qualifications," and "qualifications" are often manifested in a "diploma." If you have a "diploma," you are qualified to make a living in society, regardless of whether this diploma is matched with practical knowledge for earning a living. It seems that a diploma is just a convenient stepping stone for you to get food. Therefore, one type of criminal has increased in society: those who forge "certificates."

However, society is now at its lowest ebb. Even if you have a "diploma," you are not guaranteed a job, or even if you have the golden sign of a doctoral degree, this depressed society will "ignore" you! A company recruitment opportunity will attract thousands upon thousands of middle school and university students with diplomas, but in the end, only about ten people are hired.

What is the use of a "diploma"? If we truly want to "plead for a child," we should seek for the child a kind of learning that is closely related to the child's actual self. However, seeking knowledge does not necessarily mean going to school. What modern schools give young people, in terms of making a living, is merely applications that do not conform to the actual practice of making a living. After reading middle school books for six years, once out of school, except for one or two things that can be used slightly, everything else is a waste of time. Ask a middle school graduate to do algebra, and he has long forgotten half of it, or may even have forgotten fractions and four operations application problems! Furthermore, in terms of thinking, as Mr. Wang Jiyuan said: "The education that schools give to young people is mostly perfunctory, propaganda, deception, and empty and impractical knowledge."

We should "plead for the child" to acquire practical knowledge!

Father and Son 229

— Zhu Kang

When the snow had just stopped, a violent storm began to roar across the Trubkula Plain. The vast, boundless wilderness was covered in pure white snow, and the distant mountains and horizons were like a blanket of velvet. The sun struggled in the frozen clouds, sometimes flashing its face at the snowy ground below, and quickly withdrawing that pale light. The cold arrogantly showed its might, sealing off the entire plain. The snowflakes gradually solidified, and the wind created snow ridges on the plain by picking up snow particles. The snowfield slowly changed, rising in some places and falling in others, making the wilderness look like a vast sea of white waves.

Father Sambatu Chahan put on his rarely worn, greasy, large purple robe. Even in the gloomy weather, the oil on the robe still shimmered. He was full of joy, as if he was the happiest person in the world! Of course! His son, who had been so ill, had suddenly recovered. Anyone would be happy. The fact that his son could get better was entirely due to the divine power of the Living Buddha Norshe Khan Yan. He had made a vow to the Living Buddha, so as soon as his only son, Tobito, was well, he busied himself taking him to the Zaltu Zabu Plain to present gifts to the Living Buddha.

Although Tobito had recovered from his illness, his emaciated body from his long illness had not recovered. However, Father Sambatu Chahan paid no attention to this. He was almost driven crazy by joy. He had lived a most honest and pious life, never engaging in the slightest bit of dishonesty. Since he had made a vow to the Living Buddha, he had to fulfill it as soon as he recovered.

Early in the morning, Sambatu Chahan had carefully counted his livestock. He picked out the fattest and strongest livestock: twenty sheep, two horses, four camels, five cows, herded them together, and before it was even dawn, he took Tobito and drove the livestock away from the Trubkula Plain towards Zaltu Zabu.

Under the attack of the bitter cold, the livestock became unusually docile. Sambatu Chahan rode on horseback, holding Tobito in his arms, and the livestock obediently followed behind. More and more hoof prints were left on the snow, and the wind and waves tumbled upside down. The sheep bleated mournfully, and the horses shook the snow from their manes from time to time. Sambatu Chahan's snot dripped onto the front of his purple robe, and he only cared about looking forward, paying no attention to anything else.

Tobito's teeth were chattering from the cold:

— Dad... Dad... Cold...

— We'll be there soon. Sambatu Chahan pointed to Mount Lutisgan.

As he and the livestock rounded the foot of Mount Lutisgan, a group of young men riding horses with guns on their shoulders rushed towards them, looking like hunters. When they met, the young man leading the group reined in his horse and said respectfully to Sambatu Chahan:

— Old man! Where are you going?

— I am going to Zaltu Zabu to present gifts to the Living Buddha.

The young man smiled, very gently, without any of the rudeness of the Khalkha people. He said comfortingly

— Old man! Bandits killed our defense soldiers at Kanchi Khehamu yesterday. The lamas of the Scientific Ikchao of Zaltu Zabu are inside informants!

Sambatu Chahan was numb and didn't know what to do. He had long heard many rumors about the Living Buddha Norshe Khan Yan, and now it had become a reality! He lowered his head to look at his child, oh dear! Tobito was dead! His whole body was stiff!

— Don't worry, let's go together and drive the ×× bandits out!

Sambatu Chahan clenched his fist and let out a roar from his withered throat:

— Go and fight the ×× bandits!

Elder Sister 230

— Zhe Ren

Little Xi said to her little friends: My sister is getting married. Little Xi didn't understand what getting married meant, but since no one else's sister was getting married, it seemed that her sister was a bit different.

Her sister liked Little Xi, and Little Xi also liked her sister. When talking about people she liked with her little friends, Little Xi often left out her parents and talked about her sister. When talking about each other's sisters, Little Xi stubbornly said that her sister was the best; but Little Xi couldn't say why her sister was the best. The little friends were unwilling to admit defeat. Why wasn't their sister as good as Little Xi's sister? They were having fun playing, but they always quarreled over their sisters and broke up unhappily. Little Xi didn't win in the end, so she cried and went home to tell her sister. Her sister wiped away her tears, held her on her lap, and told a funny story. When Little Xi stopped crying and smiled, she advised her not to argue with her little friends. All sisters are good. But Little Xi was always unconvinced, and in a few days, the same thing happened again.

On the day her sister got married, Little Xi was extremely proud. Her house was wide open, and the hall was hung with lanterns and decorations. She wore a newly made robe. She stood outside the gate early in the morning, and when she saw a little friend, she boasted that her sister was getting married. Little Xi thought this was the best reason for her sister. She had finally found the answer today. The little friends were also wearing red and green clothes, and they were well-behaved, looking like they had come specifically to eat wedding candy. They were just smiling, not pouting their little lips and bickering as they usually did when talking about sisters. The little friends knew that they should be polite when they were guests. They could give many reasons to refute Little Xi, what was so special about her sister getting married? But they didn't answer Little Xi and crowded around to see the bride. This naturally made Little Xi even happier. Her sister was ultimately the best.

In the afternoon, a military band in uniform marched from outside the gate straight into the hall, with drums, trumpets, so many fun things. Little Xi and her little friends often imitated the military march in the open space, pounding their chests with their little fists as if they were playing drums, and stretching out their arms, pressing down on the air with their ten little fingers as if they were playing trumpets. At the same time, everyone imitated the sounds of various instruments, as long as they had heard them. Now that Little Xi saw so many instruments, she waved her hand, as if holding a conductor's baton, wanting to greet her little friends to practice the military march in real life. But the little friends were not as playful as usual. When the band was playing in the hall, they immediately occupied a seat. What kind of trick was this again, to watch the new official.

After doing so many novel tricks, Little Xi was simply stunned. Those little friends also looked enchanted. Everyone stood and sat politely. Finally, Little Xi's sister came out, and Little Xi looked proudly at her little friends, wanting to show that her sister was the best. But those little friends were just cheering and looking at the bride. Little Xi watched as a sedan chair hanging with tassels carried her sister away. She became anxious and wanted to chase after her, but the hall was crowded with people. She could only grab her mother's sleeve and ask, "Where is sister going?" Her mother saw that her eyes were red, as if she was about to cry, so she quickly hugged her and took her to the back room, wiped her tears like her sister, sat her on her lap, and kissed her face, saying... "Sister is getting married and going to her husband's house. Girls have to get married, and you will be carried away in a fancy sedan chair in the future."

Little Xi just opened her eyes wide. Getting married was originally this kind of thing. Then, she asked her mother, when would her sister come back?

In a few days, her sister came back, and the new official also accompanied her. Little Xi became angry when she saw the strange man. He had taken her sister away. In the evening, her brother-in-law left, but her sister stayed at home. Little Xi was so happy that she twisted her sister around, wanting her to tell stories. But when she saw that her sister's eyes were red from crying, she slowly retreated into her mother's arms, watching suspiciously. She felt that there were too many things she didn't understand. Why did her sister cry when she came back home?

Her mother kissed her face again and said, "Your brother-in-law is not good and bullied your sister." Little Xi stretched out her little fist and answered her mother, I will beat the brother-in-law, and don't let him come again in the future, and my sister shouldn't go to his house again. But her mother shook her head, and Little Xi felt very disappointed. Although she had such a best sister, there were really too many things she didn't understand.

Lantern Festival 231

— Fang Zhou

As usual, after the thirteenth day of the lunar new year in the village, there would be a lively scene again; the east village would have horse lanterns, and the west village would have dragon dances. Those farmers who had worked hard for a year would take these few days to revel as much as possible, to relieve the breath that had been oppressed by life for so long. Even the women and children would run around day and night.

San He heard in the teahouse in town today that Shi Ren Tou was going to have horse lanterns again this year, and he was as happy as a child, jumping to tell his wife the news he brought back from the teahouse:

"Shi Ren Tou's horse lanterns are going to be held for sure. I heard that the date has been chosen, it's the sixteenth of the lunar month, the day after tomorrow, the sixteenth of the lunar month is the day after tomorrow."

"What's the excitement about other people's dragon lanterns and horse lanterns!" San He's wife glanced at him and replied coldly, still mending her shoe soles.

Unexpectedly, his joy only got him a cold blast from his wife, and he felt disappointed; but thinking about his own excitement at the time, it was really too silly and ridiculous, no wonder he would run into her nail.

He sat sullenly on a low stool and finished that Chimei brand cigarette in one breath, then lit another one. He thought: The horse lanterns here used to start every year from the thirteenth or fourteenth of the lunar month and would last until the end of the month, but since the countryside suffered from floods, droughts, wars, bandit disasters, and the heavy oppression of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies, the villagers often found it difficult to even make a living, so where would they get the interest to start any lantern festivals? The horse lanterns in Shi Ren Tou, which used to be very famous, had not been out for three or four years; and he himself had played in those horse lanterns. This year, it was rare that someone was reviving these horse lanterns that had been suspended for three or four years, so naturally I should play some role, fortune-telling, palm reading, offering vegetarian meals, anything will do, in short, just need to act alike, say it loosely. ... (To be continued)

Broadcast Programs

Storytelling 232

Cai Xiaofang's Record of Retribution

China and the West (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening "Spring Outing Song"

Soft willow catkins rise pale yellow. Peach blossoms compete with new makeup. The spring scenery bothers people, they can't sleep. A branch of red apricot extends beyond the east wall. Decorating the spring scenery with warmth. Red fat and green thin compete in strange fragrance. Every leaf and flower is picturesque. Orioles sing, swallows laugh, butterflies and bees flit. Even more joyous, grass and trees meet spring and are healthy. The wind awakens the yellow beam every morning. A view of half the plain is beautiful. The branches of beautiful flowers often accompany Lagerstroemia indica. Friends go on spring outings. The welcoming grass brushes the transverse embankment. Still more joyous, the willows want to sprout and the peaches want to bloom. There is a deep feeling that requires comparison. One must know that the best scenery is originally in spring. Natural paintings are in the riverside village. Wait until the third month of the spring scenery is deepest. A thousand reds and ten thousand purples are even more fragrant. However, the same beauty has several kinds of views. Let me distinguish the details. Some are young women thinking of spring, their hearts are confused. The sleepy weather is even more茫茫. Occasionally seeing green willows on the street. They say, I hope my husband will be ennobled. Some are young ladies and famous women in their boudoirs. In the deep boudoir, they quietly embroider mandarin ducks. Suddenly feeling that the bothersome spring scenery has arrived. They are tired of books and have a long afternoon dream. Some are couples with deep affection, looking at the beautiful scenery with affection. They go on spring outings in the suburbs. They speak of their deep love and affection. Some are men of letters and poets who accompany each other. In the apricot blossom village, they share wine. Some are widows whose thoughts of their husbands are painful. They lazily look at the spring scenery and lie in their beds. Although one kind of sorrow cannot be forgotten. How can they face the disturbing spring dream? Therefore, the spring scenery is originally the same. Some people are happy and laughing, some are sad. Talking about it is harmless.

Nonsense 235

— (Blow)

For the past eighteen years, no German soldiers have been seen along the Rhine. The other day, German troops marched into the city of Frankfurt. Tens of millions of people cheered in unison, and some were so happy that they wept. The residents of Bonn even broke through the barriers of the advancing troops and hung garlands around the soldiers' necks. Tan Lao San said that this is like country people not recognizing the revolving lantern, saying, "Here it comes again," "Here it comes again." Zhu commented that the first "Here it comes again" is when the German troops marched into the Rhine, and the second "Here it comes again" is probably the beginning of the second great war.

The German troops suddenly marched into the Rhine, and France is using all its strength to resist Germany. Diplomacy and military affairs are being pursued simultaneously, and the situation is very tense. Tan Lao San said, "Pursuing simultaneously will scare the old lady to death. The situation is tense, a big war is about to break out. If a character-splitting fortune teller sees it, it must be more bad luck than good."

The Sino-Western Radio Station will add a weekly "Cartoon Lecture" every Saturday afternoon at 4:00 PM, starting from the 14th of this month, hosted by Mr. Zhang Yizhang. It is also said that any questions regarding cartoons can be sent to the station, requesting Mr. Zhang to answer them.

The Zhi Ming Music and Singing Society will broadcast a special program every Sunday from 12:00 PM to 1:00 PM on the Yadong Radio Station. It is also said that the society has prepared many copies of the "Youth Song" to be distributed to all sectors of society. Those who request by mail (no postage required) will be sent a copy immediately. (Onlooker)

Ming Mei: The song "I Really Failed You" written by pianist Mr. Zhou Mingyuan has been rehearsed several times and deemed very pleasing to the ear. The simplified score has now been printed. Those who wish to obtain the music sheet, please enclose two cents postage and send it to the Ming Mei Troupe, Lilli Radio Station, No. 9 Anyi Village, Xizang Road, Shanghai, and it will be sent without delay.

The Modern Society, after being born, has not yet reached its first month and has already died prematurely, making it the shortest-lived in the singing world.

Movie News

"Tian Lun" Goes to America 239

Since its release, "Tian Lun" has been publicly performed in various places, and both its critical acclaim and box office success have been outstanding. It has been called "the pinnacle of the national-made silent film era," a statement that most people who have seen the film do not deny.

But the film has not only received praise from the Chinese people, but also international attention, which is also noteworthy. In Europe, the film will be screened in theaters in various places. Recently, Paramount Pictures in the United States has telegraphed Lianhua, requesting the rights to release and distribute the film in the United States, and the terms have already been agreed upon.

In the narrow Chinese film market, it is a gratifying thing that "Tian Lun" can be promoted to Europe and America!

How Many Jokes in "Guo Se Tian Xiang"? 240

The Shanghai Film Company's great sound film "Guo Se Tian Xiang" will soon be publicly screened at the Carlton, starring Dan Erchun, Bai Hong, and Bai Yan. It features wanderers in a bustling city, a righteous singing girl, a police officer who arrests the wrong thief, a manager full of embarrassing behavior, a beautiful female clerk in a shoe store, a singing salesman from a confectionery company, a musician upstairs in a tailor shop, and a young man who falls asleep as soon as he hears about national affairs. The performances are extremely interesting, and the positive intentions are hidden in the jokes, showing the painstaking efforts of the writers and directors.

Entertainment Weekly Pictorial Published 241

The Entertainment Weekly, which combines film, broadcasting, drama, dance, and literature into one, has substantial content, lively arrangement, and is extremely popular among readers. The tenth issue of the second volume of this publication has been published today. The cover features beautiful steel engravings of Ms. Qi Nian and Ms. Xu Lai, South China artists. The text includes "Anecdotes of National Athletes and Flowers of South China," "Modern Social Dance," "Achievements in Broadcasting in the Past Two Years," "Chaliapin's Short History," "Han Lan Heng and Luo Shan's Ill-Fated Romance," "Fort Lamartine Hates Being a Screen Lover," "Shao Zuiweng's Way to Make Money," etc., which are exceptionally wonderful. Each issue retails for five cents. The Photography Pictorial published by the Photography Pictorial Society is the only publication in the country that studies photography. Each issue has articles selected by famous photographers and a selection of world photography masterpieces. The text includes "Principles of Composition," "Photography in the Animal Kingdom," "Factor Development Method," "Self-Made Method of Enhanced Development," "Winter Photography with a Small Camera," "Outdoor Portrait Photography," "Development in Cold Weather," etc. Each issue retails for one dime, and it will be sent immediately with one dime postage.

Grand Cathay Ballroom Opens 242

The Grand Cathay Ballroom, which has been under preparation for a long time and was completed today with the highest decorations and artistic furnishings of 1936, is scheduled to have the opening ceremony performed by Ms. Wu Lizhu, the Eastern Female Fairbanks, at 4:00 PM this afternoon. It is said that all the interior decorations of the ballroom were planned by American design experts, and tea dances will be held daily, with famous dance stars accompanying the dance. All male and female guests will be given refreshments. Today, there will also be gifts from major manufacturers. A particularly famous and surprising performance newly arrived from Europe will be presented. It is expected that there will be a lot of excitement at the corner of Avenue Joffre and Rue Chu Pao San this afternoon.
